[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I have created for this workplace environment survey is as follows, where each element in 'TF_QUESTIONS' array represents one specific multiple-choice or single choice type of the same format. ```json
{    "data": {        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [            {"CODE":"1","NAME" : "[WORKPLACE ENVIRONMENT SURVEY] QPS",                "__TYPE__ID230674598DCAEBAFDAAFDFADDDFCBBFFCBCBDBCEADEDADEFGFCDDCEDFEEEEF1GHIJIHKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ","_TF": {                    "_TITLE__ID230674598DCAEBAFDAAFDFADDDFCBBFFCBCBDBCEADEDADEFGFCDDCEDFEEEEF1GHIJIHKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ_ANSWERS": [                        {"CODE":"","NAME" : "Strongly Agree",                "__TYPE__ID230674598DCAEBAFDAAFDFADDDFCBBFFCBCBDBCEADEDADEFGFCDDCEDFEEEEF1GHIJIHKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ_ANSWER": "This workplace is a pleasant place to be in", "__TYPE__ID230674598DCAEBAFDAAFDFADDDFCBBFFCBCBDBCEADEDADEFGFCDDCEDFEEEEF1GHIJIHKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ_DISPLAYORDER": 1}

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

Generate me a questionnaire on Career path with 10 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I have chosen for this career-path focused, ten item long Questionaire is as follows - A single JSON object containing one property 'data' which in turn contains another Property called "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES" that holds an array of questionnaires. Each element (Questionnaire) inside the TF\_ QUESTATIONAIRE Array has several properties such
- CODE: Unique identifier for each Questionaire, ex - CP105678GHJKL or something like this in string format; NAME : The name of that questionairre. It can be anything related to the topic and informative about what is being asked through it such as "Career Path" here ; TYPE\_ID: Int value which will remain 3 for all Questionnaire types,
- _TF_QUESTIONS Array containing multiple Objects of Questions in that particular questionairre. Each object has several properties like CODE : Unique identifier string format similar to the one we used with QUIZ ABOUT YOU but this time specific and unique; NAME: The actual Question content, TYPE\_ID (int) This value will vary depending on whether it is Multiple Choice or Single choice etc.
- _TF_ANSWERS Array containing multiple Objects of answers in that particular question if there are any available for a given QUESTION otherwise null and the ANSR Property which contains actual answer string format; DISPLAY\_ORDER Int value to order questions based on this number from 1st one, second two etc.
- In addition I have added some properties like MULTIPLE_CHOICE or SINGEL CHOIcE with boolean values True and False respectively if that question is multiple choice true otherwise false; LONG\_DESCRIPTION : A detailed explanation of the Question in string format to make it more interactive for users.
- And a property called "SUGGESTED_ANSWERS" which contains array object having max 4 items with their codes and names as properties, This will help user by suggesting them correct code while answering questions if they want; I have also used different type of answers to make it more interactive for example N/A or Not Applicable etc.
- And finally a property called "IS\_REQUIRED" which is boolean value true false respectively indicating that the question should be answered and not left blank otherwise, This will help user by suggesting them correct code while answering questions if they want; I have also used different type of answers to make it more interactive for example N/A or Not Applicable etc.
Below you can find JSON formatted Questionnaire on Career path with 10 Questions - Please note that all the above mentioned properties are not necessarily needed in every question and some questions might be missing few things but I have tried my best to make it more interactive for users by using different type of answers, suggestions etc.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I will use for this learner's post-course evaluation is as follows - there are eight main categories, each containing one or more prompts to elicit specific information. Each prompt has an associated answer type (either single select option / multiple selections allowed).
Questions about course content and material: 1) "How would you rate the overall quality of this year's learning materials?" with a five-star scale for answers, where one star means very poor; two to three stars indicate average or mixed feelings towards it while four starts mean good but not excellent. Five Stars represent an outstanding course content experience in your opinion.; 2) "Which specific topic(s)/learning material do you think needs improvement?" - This question allows learners' detailed feedback on particular topics that may have been problematic, and they can select multiple options if necessary;
Questions about the format of delivery: a). Teaching methodology – Is there anything special/unique regarding this course? Please specify what makes it stand out from others. b) Preferred medium for learning - What type(s)/format (video lectures / text-based content etc.) do you prefer to learn best and why?;
Questions about the teacher: a). Teacher'S ENGAGEMENT – Did they make an effort throughout their teaching session? Please specify areas where improvement is needed. b) Perception of Tutor - Were your expectations met regarding personality, knowledge level & communication skills when delivering course content to students?. Rate them on scale 1-5;
Questions about learner's engagement: a). Peer Interaction – How valuable was interaction with classmates during this session? Please rate it from extremely useful (score=4) downwards. b ) Self Assessment - In your opinion, how much did you learn and grew as an individual after attending these sessions compared to before starting them?. Rate yourself on scale 1-5;
Questions about course relevance: a). Relevancy of Course – Is the content relevant in today's world? If not specifically then what improvements would make it more applicable. b) Suggested Changes - What changes or additions do you think should be included to enhance its effectiveness and applicability for future learners?.
Questions about course impact: a). Personal Impact of Course – How has this session affected your life personally? Please share any anecdotes if possible, as it will help us understand the value derived from attending. b) Recommendation - Would you recommend others to attend same/similar sessions based on what was learned here?.
Questions about course satisfaction: a). Course Satisfaction – Were your needs met satisfactorily during this session? Please specify areas where improvement is needed and those that were perfect, so we can continue delivering high-quality learning experiences. b) Comparison with Previous Sessions - How does it compare to previous sessions you have attended in terms of quality & impact?. Rate them on scale 1: not satisfied at all; two – somewhat dissatisfied but willingness for improvement is there till four stars, which means completely content and five starts that represent a highly satisfactory experience.
Questions about course useful life :- How long did you think the knowledge gained from this session would remain relevant in your field of work? Please specify areas where it may become obsolete or need frequent updates; 2) Would You like to stay connected with Us and our other courses if yes how many days a week is suitable for that.
Questions about course difficulty: - How difficult was the content on scale one-to five, please select according your comfort level? If you find it tough then we need some modification in delivery or timing of concept; 3) Would like to give us feedback if yes how many students are good and bad for that because sometimes even a single student can make our day.
Questions about course accessibility: - How accessible was the content on scale one-to five, please select according your comfort level? If you find it tough then we need some modification in delivery or timing of concept; 4) Would You like to share this knowledge with others if yes how many days a week is suitable for that.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I will follow for creating this JSON object is as follows - there are several properties under 'data' which itself exists within an outermost curly brackets (indicating that it’s indeed the root of our questionnaire). Within data, we have a property called "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES" and its value will be another array.
This particular element in this TF\_ QUES TONAIRE Sarray is an object containing several properties - CODE (string), NAME(String) which should indicate it’s technology access questionnaire, TYPE ID as 3 because we are creating a rating type of questions and lastly the _TF_QUESTIONS array.
Within this "_ TF QUES TONAIRE Sarray", there will be only nine objects - representing each individual query/question in our Access to Technology & Tools questionnaire, with their respective properties: CODE(string), NAME (String) which should indicate the content of every specific questions and its DISPLAY ORDER.
Within these 9 elements inside "_ TF_QUESTIONS" array there will be no property called 'ANSWERS' because we want to get user engagement by using creative syntax for all our queries/questions - this means that each question is inherently an object with multiple properties and not just a simple string.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100021
     - Topic: Health and Safety Measures
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

 Explanation: Below you will find an example JSON format for generating 'INTERNAL_MOBILITY' topic in Human Resource Management field, containing seven (multi-type)questions and their respective answers. The data array contains a single property called TF\_QUESTIONNAIRES which includes the following information about each questionnaire:
CODE - unique code of that specific survey or form; NAME – name/title given to this particular set in order for it be easily identified by users, TYPE_ID- type identifier. Here we have chosen a mix and match types like 3 (rating),5(reordering) &6-(distributing weights across several items).
Please note that each question has its own code as well to make sure no two questions are the same within one survey or form, also for easy reference in case of any changes. The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.

 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

               _TTF ANSWERS array for this multiple choice rating type question object has following properties:    "AN SWER": String value representing a particular answer to be given when using Question Code.                "CODE": String value representing a unique code for this particular Question. This MUST be UNIQUE within your system to avoid any confusion or conflicts when collecting data from multiple sources into the same database,   	"NAME ":  The actual text of each question is stored in NAME property as string and it should not contain semicolon ";",

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I will use for this 'OnBoarding Questionniare' is as follows - there are seven different sections (questions) in it, each represented under the '_TF_QUESTIONS’ property of an object. Each section has a unique code and name that describes what type/format question they represent; their display order on screen or preference can also be set using 'DISPLAY ORDER' attribute - for example if you want to make this survey look more like conversation then first questions should have lower number than the later ones in terms of DISPLAT_ORDER. And finally, each section has a list (array) that includes all possible answers and their code under '_TF\_ANSWERS’ property; these codes can be used for analysis purposes or even to calculate scores based on provided set values if needed!

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100042
     - Topic: Recognition and Rewards
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Recognition and Rewards with 8 questions

-------------------

 Explanation: The structure I will use is as follows - there are eight different types, or categories if you prefer of recognition-related statements that an employee can agree (or disagree) to varying degrees. Each statement has a code for internal tracking purposes ('CODE') and the text itself which includes spaces so it reads better than just being in all caps with no punctuation at end 'NAME'. The type id is 8 because I am using this format of question, but any other number can be used if you want to use another style. Each statement also has a display order ('DISPLAY_ORDER') which determines the sequence they appear and whether there are multiple choice options for answers or just one answer as it does not make sense in certain contexts (either through '_TF\_ANSWERS' array of objects with 'TYPE ID = 1,2', OR if only a single option is to be allowed then that will simply exist without being inside an object).

[LLM ANSWER]

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions

[LLM ANSWER]
 Explanation: The structure I will use for this workplace environment survey is as follows - there are seven different topics that make up our 'questions' array, each represented in an object and containing the following properties necessary to describe it. Each topic has a unique code (CODE), content or question text displayed on screen ('NAME'), type of answer expected from user with IDs corresponding directly 1-6 as described above under QUESTION_TYPES section - this is not necessarily used but gives more flexibility if another system needs the data, and then 'DISPLAY\_ORDER' which will allow us to order questions in a specific way for better UX.
Another array of objects (_TF\_{PICKER} or _TFSINGLE) exists within each question representing different answer choices - this is optional but if included also contains the ANSWERS as strings and not IDs unless using another system that requires them, in which case you can use 1-5 to represent STRONGLY\_AGREE etc.
The seven topics I have chosen are: 'OPENNESS', describing how open a person'is towards new experiences; this question type is rated out of five (TYPE=3) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongest agreement to disagreement.
Next comes the topic on whether someone feels comfortable at work or not - again a simple yes/no choice but presented as three options so user can select 'NEUTRAL' if they wish (TYPE=2) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-3 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.
Next up is the topic of office temperature - this time allowing users more granularity by providing them six options ranging between 'TOO\_COLD' through a neutral option (TYPE=6) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.
Then we move onto QUIETNESS - do people feel comfortable speaking up about issues they perceive as important? Again allowing users more granularity by providing them six options ranging between 'TOO\_LOUD' through a neutral option (TYPE=6) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.
Next is LIGHT - how well lit does someone feel their environment should be? Again allowing users more granularity by providing them six options ranging between 'TOO\_DARK' through a neutral option (TYPE=6) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.
Next we consider whether the person is able easily understand other people at work or not - again allowing users more granularity by providing them six options ranging between 'DIFFICULT\_TOO' through a neutral option (TYPE=6) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.
Finally we consider the topic of how much someone enjoys their current role - again allowing users more granularity by providing them six options ranging between 'VERY\_MUCH' through a neutral option (TYPE=6) and displayed using an ordered list for better UX design, with display order 1-5 in sequence from strongly agree to disagree.

               _TFSINGLE">       },   {"CODE\":«: «OPENNESS», "NAME»:"How open are you to new experiences?",    TYPE_ID":3,        "_TFQUESTIONS":"[{"DISPLAYORDER"1,"ANSWERS"\["STRONGLY\_AGREE"," AGREEE\"],
               _TFSINGLE">       },   {"CODE\":«: «COMFORTABLE», "NAME»:"Do you feel comfortable in the office?",    TYPE_ID":2,        "_TFQUESTIONS":"[{"DISPLAYORDER"1,"ANSWERS"\["YES","NO"],
               _TFSINGLE">       },   {"CODE\":«: «OFFICE\_TEMPERATURE», "NAME»:"How would you describe the temperature of your office?",    TYPE_ID":6,        "_TFQUESTIONS":"[{"DISPLAYORDER"1,"ANSWERS"\["TOO COLD"," TOOC OLD"],
               _TFSINGLE">       },   {"CODE\":«: «QUALITY», "NAME»:"How would you rate the quality of interaction with others?",    TYPE_ID":6,        "_TFQUESTIONS":"[{"DISPLAYORDER"1,"ANSWERS"\["TOO LOUD"," TOOC OLD"],
